 K = 8192
 N = 4096
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
+B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+C_RANGE_BYTES = M * N * 2
+
 
 @substrate.jit
 def gemm_kernel(
-    A: S.Tensor((2048, 8192), S.bf16),
-    B: S.Tensor((8192, 4096), S.bf16),
-    C: S.Tensor((2048, 4096), S.bf16),
+    A: S.Tensor((M * K,), S.bf16),
+    B: S.Tensor((K * N,), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M * N,), S.bf16),
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp >> 1
+    warp_col = warp & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(A_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(B_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            frag = tid
+            wave_row_id = frag >> 6
+            row_in_wave = frag & 31
+            chunk = (frag >> 5) & 1
+            global_row = block_row + wave_row_id * 32 + row_in_wave
+            global_col = k_tile * BLOCK_K + chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_row * K + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
 
+            lane_lo = row_in_wave
+            lane_hi = row_in_wave + 32
+            base = chunk * 4
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + i] = vals[i]
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + i] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            frag = tid - 128
+            wave_col_id = frag >> 6
+            row_k = frag >> 3
+            col_chunk = frag & 7
+            global_k = k_tile * BLOCK_K + row_k
+            global_col = block_col + wave_col_id * 32 + col_chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_k * N + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+            lane_group = (row_k >> 2) * 32
+            slot = (row_k & 3) + ((row_k >> 3) * 4)
+            for i in S.range(8):
+                b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_group + col_chunk * 8 + i, slot] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        b_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        for i in S.range(8):
+            a_pack[i] = a_shared[warp_row, lane, i]
+            b_pack[i] = b_shared[warp_col, lane, i]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    out_col = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane & 31)
+    row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32 + ((lane >> 5) * 4)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = row_base + (i >> 2) * 8 + (i & 3)
+        C[out_row * N + out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._grid = ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):

+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

 N = 4096

+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4

+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp >> 1
+    warp_col = warp & 1
 
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
 
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(A_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(B_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            frag = tid
+            wave_row_id = frag >> 6
+            row_in_wave = frag & 31
+            chunk = (frag >> 5) & 1
+            global_row = block_row + wave_row_id * 32 + row_in_wave
+            global_col = k_tile * BLOCK_K + chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_row * K + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+            lane_lo = row_in_wave
+            lane_hi = row_in_wave + 32
+            base = chunk * 4
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + i] = vals[i]
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + i] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            frag = tid - 128
+            wave_col_id = frag >> 6
+            row_k = frag >> 3
+            col_chunk = frag & 7
+            global_k = k_tile * BLOCK_K + row_k

+            elem_offset = global_k * N + global_col

+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+

+            slot = (row_k & 3) + ((row_k >> 3) * 4)
+            for i in S.range(8):
+                b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_group + col_chunk * 8 + i, slot] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        b_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        for i in S.range(8):
+            a_pack[i] = a_shared[warp_row, lane, i]
+            b_pack[i] = b_shared[warp_col, lane, i]
+        a_words = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        b_words = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((4,), S.u32))
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = row_base + (i >> 2) * 8 + (i & 3)
+        C[out_row * N + out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+

+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])

+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+            lane_lo = row_in_wave
+            lane_hi = row_in_wave + 32
+            base = chunk * 4
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + i] = vals[i]
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + i] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            frag = tid - 128
+            wave_col_id = frag >> 6
+            row_k = frag >> 3
+            col_chunk = frag & 7
+            global_k = k_tile * BLOCK_K + row_k
+            global_col = block_col + wave_col_id * 32 + col_chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_k * N + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+            lane_group = (row_k >> 2) * 32
+            slot = (row_k & 3) + ((row_k >> 3) * 4)
+            for i in S.range(8):
+                b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_group + col_chunk * 8 + i, slot] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
 
+        a_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        b_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        for i in S.range(8):
+            a_pack[i] = a_shared[warp_row, lane, i]
+            b_pack[i] = b_shared[warp_col, lane, i]
+        a0 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        a1 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        b0 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        b1 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a0[i, 0] = a_pack[i]
+            a1[i, 0] = a_pack[i + 4]
+            b0[i, 0] = b_pack[i]
+            b1[i, 0] = b_pack[i + 4]
 
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a0, b0, acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1, b1, acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    out_col = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane & 31)
+    row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32 + ((lane >> 5) * 4)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = row_base + (i >> 2) * 8 + (i & 3)
+        C[out_row * N + out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._grid = ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+            global_col = k_tile * BLOCK_K + chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_row * K + global_col

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+            lane_lo = row_in_wave
+            lane_hi = row_in_wave + 32
+            base = chunk * 4
+            for i in S.range(4):
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + i] = vals[i]
+                a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + i] = vals[i + 4]
+        else:
+            frag = tid - 128
+            wave_col_id = frag >> 6
+            row_k = frag >> 3
+            col_chunk = frag & 7
+            global_k = k_tile * BLOCK_K + row_k
+            global_col = block_col + wave_col_id * 32 + col_chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_k * N + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            vals = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16))
+
+            lane_group = (row_k >> 2) * 32
+            slot = (row_k & 3) + ((row_k >> 3) * 4)
+            for i in S.range(8):
+                b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_group + col_chunk * 8 + i, slot] = vals[i]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
 
+        a_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        b_pack = S.make_local((8,), S.bf16)
+        for i in S.range(8):
+            a_pack[i] = a_shared[warp_row, lane, i]
+            b_pack[i] = b_shared[warp_col, lane, i]
+        a0 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        a1 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        b0 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        b1 = S.make_local((4, 1), S.bf16)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a0[i, 0] = a_pack[i]
+            a1[i, 0] = a_pack[i + 4]
+            b0[i, 0] = b_pack[i]
+            b1[i, 0] = b_pack[i + 4]
 
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a0, b0, acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1, b1, acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    out_col = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane & 31)
+    row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32 + ((lane >> 5) * 4)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = row_base + (i >> 2) * 8 + (i & 3)
+        C[out_row * N + out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
+        self._grid = ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
-        A = A.contiguous()
-        B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
+            raise ValueError(f"Expected A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
+            raise ValueError(f"Expected bf16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}")
+
+        A_flat = A.contiguous().view(-1)
+        B_flat = B.contiguous().view(-1)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        C_flat = C.view(-1)
+        gemm_kernel[lambda: self._grid](A_flat, B_flat, C_flat)
         return C

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

codex
The clean path is to transpose `B` once in `forward()` so both operands present contiguous K-major rows to the kernel. That lets me stage both `A` and `B` into the same packed LDS fragment layout the MFMA op expects, without the lowering problems from repacking strided B data inside the kernel.
apply patch

+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

 N = 4096
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
+B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+C_RANGE_BYTES = M * N * 2

 def gemm_kernel(
-    A: S.Tensor((2048, 8192), S.bf16),

 ):

+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp >> 1
+    warp_col = warp & 1

+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(A_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    bt_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(BT, S.convert(B_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
 
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            frag = tid
+            wave_row_id = frag >> 6
+            row_in_wave = frag & 31
+            chunk = (frag >> 5) & 1
+            global_row = block_row + wave_row_id * 32 + row_in_wave
+            global_col = k_tile * BLOCK_K + chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_row * K + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            lane_lo = row_in_wave
+            lane_hi = row_in_wave + 32
+            base = chunk * 2
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            frag = tid - 128
+            wave_col_id = frag >> 6
+            col_in_wave = frag & 31
+            chunk = (frag >> 5) & 1
+            global_col = block_col + wave_col_id * 32 + col_in_wave

+            b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_hi, base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_hi, base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        b_words = S.make_local((4,), S.u32)
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_words[i] = a_shared[warp_row, lane, i]
+            b_words[i] = b_shared[warp_col, lane, i]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+    row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32 + ((lane >> 5) * 4)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = row_base + (i >> 2) * 8 + (i & 3)
+        C[out_row * N + out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
+

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch
+
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(
+    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
+    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    c = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c)
+    C[lane] = c
+
+
+def pack_pairs(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    words = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).view(*x.shape[:-1], x.shape[-1] // 2, 2)
+    lo = words[..., 0].to(torch.int32) & 0xFFFF
+    hi = words[..., 1].to(torch.int32) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def launch(A_vals: torch.Tensor, B_vals: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    C = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device=A_vals.device)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](pack_pairs(A_vals), pack_pairs(B_vals), C)
+    return C
+
+
+def main():
+    device = "cuda"
+    ones4 = torch.ones((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+
+    row_masks = []
+    for a_slot in range(256):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(A, ones4)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        row_masks.append(mask)
+
+    col_masks = []
+    for b_slot in range(256):
+        B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+        C = launch(ones4, B)
+        mask = (C.cpu() != 0).view(-1).to(torch.int32)
+        col_masks.append(mask)
+
+    row_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(row_masks):
+        row_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    col_groups = {}
+    for idx, mask in enumerate(col_masks):
+        col_groups.setdefault(tuple(mask.tolist()), []).append(idx)
+
+    print("row groups", len(row_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in row_groups.values())[-4:])
+    print("col groups", len(col_groups), sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[:4], sorted(len(v) for v in col_groups.values())[-4:])
+
+    row_keys = list(row_groups.keys())
+    col_keys = list(col_groups.keys())
+
+    # Build output mapping from row-mask/col-mask intersections.
+    out_map = {}
+    for r_id, r_key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        r_mask = torch.tensor(r_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+        for c_id, c_key in enumerate(col_keys):
+            c_mask = torch.tensor(c_key, dtype=torch.int32)
+            inter = torch.nonzero((r_mask & c_mask) != 0, as_tuple=False).view(-1)
+            if inter.numel() != 1:
+                print("bad intersection", r_id, c_id, inter.numel())
+                return
+            out_map[(r_id, c_id)] = int(inter.item())
+
+    # Recover k labels by pairing one row-group with one col-group.
+    ref_row_slots = row_groups[row_keys[0]]
+    ref_col_slots = col_groups[col_keys[0]]
+    a_k = {}
+    b_k = {}
+    out_index = out_map[(0, 0)]
+    for k_id, a_slot in enumerate(ref_row_slots):
+        A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+        A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+        matched = None
+        for b_slot in ref_col_slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+            if C[out_index] != 0:
+                matched = b_slot
+                break
+        if matched is None:
+            print("no match for", a_slot)
+            return
+        a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+        b_k[matched] = k_id
+
+    # Extend k labels to every row/col group by matching against the reference group.
+    for slots in row_groups.values():
+        for a_slot in slots:
+            A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+            r_mask = row_masks[a_slot]
+            r_id = row_keys.index(tuple(r_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(r_id, 0)]
+            for b_slot, k_id in b_k.items():
+                B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    a_k[a_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    for slots in col_groups.values():
+        for b_slot in slots:
+            B = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+            B.view(-1)[b_slot] = 1
+            c_mask = col_masks[b_slot]
+            c_id = col_keys.index(tuple(c_mask.tolist()))
+            out_index = out_map[(0, c_id)]
+            for a_slot, k_id in a_k.items():
+                A = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device)
+                A.view(-1)[a_slot] = 1
+                C = launch(A, B).cpu().view(-1)
+                if C[out_index] != 0:
+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

 N = 4096
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
+B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+C_RANGE_BYTES = M * N * 2

+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)

+            wave_row_id = frag >> 6
+            row_in_wave = frag & 31
+            chunk = (frag >> 5) & 1
+            global_row = block_row + wave_row_id * 32 + row_in_wave
+            global_col = k_tile * BLOCK_K + chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_row * K + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            lane_lo = row_in_wave
+            lane_hi = row_in_wave + 32

+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + 0] = packed[2]

+                    b_k[b_slot] = k_id
+                    break
+
+    row_id_by_slot = {}
+    for r_id, key in enumerate(row_keys):
+        for slot in row_groups[key]:
+            row_id_by_slot[slot] = r_id
+    col_id_by_slot = {}
+    for c_id, key in enumerate(col_keys):
+        for slot in col_groups[key]:
+            col_id_by_slot[slot] = c_id
+
+    print("A mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(row_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e], a_k[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("B mapping")
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [(b_k[4 * lane + e], col_id_by_slot[4 * lane + e]) for e in range(4)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+    print("C mapping")
+    inv_out = {v: k for k, v in out_map.items()}
+    for lane in range(64):
+        vals = [inv_out[16 * lane + e] for e in range(16)]
+        print(lane, vals)
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

 K = 8192
 N = 4096
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = 256
+A_RANGE_BYTES = M * K * 2
+B_RANGE_BYTES = K * N * 2
+C_RANGE_BYTES = M * N * 2
+
 
 @substrate.jit
 def gemm_kernel(
-    A: S.Tensor((2048, 8192), S.bf16),
-    B: S.Tensor((8192, 4096), S.bf16),
-    C: S.Tensor((2048, 4096), S.bf16),
+    A: S.Tensor((M * K,), S.bf16),
+    BT: S.Tensor((N * K,), S.bf16),
+    C: S.Tensor((M * N,), S.bf16),
 ):
-    for i in S.range(M):
-        for j in S.range(N):
-            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-            for kk in S.range(K):
-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp >> 1
+    warp_col = warp & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(A_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+    bt_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(BT, S.convert(B_RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K // BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            frag = tid
+            wave_row_id = frag >> 6
+            row_in_wave = frag & 31
+            chunk = (frag >> 5) & 1
+            global_row = block_row + wave_row_id * 32 + row_in_wave
+            global_col = k_tile * BLOCK_K + chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_row * K + global_col
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            lane_lo = row_in_wave
+            lane_hi = row_in_wave + 32
+            base = chunk * 2
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + 0] = packed[0]
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_lo, base + 1] = packed[1]
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + 0] = packed[2]
+            a_shared[wave_row_id, lane_hi, base + 1] = packed[3]
+        else:
+            frag = tid - 128
+            wave_col_id = frag >> 6
+            col_in_wave = frag & 31
+            chunk = (frag >> 5) & 1
+            global_col = block_col + wave_col_id * 32 + col_in_wave
+            global_k = k_tile * BLOCK_K + chunk * 8
+            elem_offset = global_col * K + global_k
+            byte_offset = S.convert(elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(bt_rsrc, zero, byte_offset, 0)
+            lane_lo = col_in_wave
+            lane_hi = col_in_wave + 32
+            base = chunk * 2
+            b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_lo, base + 0] = packed[0]
+            b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_lo, base + 1] = packed[1]
+            b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_hi, base + 0] = packed[2]
+            b_shared[wave_col_id, lane_hi, base + 1] = packed[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_words = a_shared[warp_row, lane]
+        b_words = b_shared[warp_col, lane]
+        a_frag = S.view(a_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    out_col = block_col + warp_col * 32 + (lane & 31)
+    row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32 + ((lane >> 5) * 4)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out_row = row_base + (i >> 2) * 8 + (i & 3)
+        C[out_row * N + out_col] = S.convert(acc[i], S.bf16)
